["Ispell PODs" cperl-pod-spell
(or
(get-text-property
(point-min)
'in-pod)
(<
(progn
(and cperl-syntaxify-for-menu
(cperl-update-syntaxification
(point-max)
(point-max)))
(next-single-property-change
(point-min)
'in-pod nil
(point-max)))
(point-max)))]
["Ispell HERE-DOCs" cperl-here-doc-spell
(<
(progn
(and cperl-syntaxify-for-menu
(cperl-update-syntaxification
(point-max)
(point-max)))
(next-single-property-change
(point-min)
'here-doc-group nil
(point-max)))
(point-max))]
["Narrow to this HERE-DOC" cperl-narrow-to-here-doc
(eq 'here-doc
(progn
(and cperl-syntaxify-for-menu
(cperl-update-syntaxification
(point)
(point)))
(get-text-property
(point)
'syntax-type)))]
["Select this HERE-DOC or POD section" cperl-select-this-pod-or-here-doc
(memq
(progn
(and cperl-syntaxify-for-menu
(cperl-update-syntaxification
(point)
(point)))
(get-text-property
(point)
'syntax-type))
'(here-doc pod))]

(memq gnus-gcc-externalize-attachments
'(all t nil))))

'(all t nil)))

["Everything"
(if
(eq idlwave-shell-show-commands 'everything)
(progn
(setq idlwave-shell-show-commands
(get 'idlwave-shell-show-commands 'last-val))
(put 'idlwave-shell-show-commands 'last-val nil))
(put 'idlwave-shell-show-commands 'last-val idlwave-shell-show-commands)
(setq idlwave-shell-show-commands 'everything))
:style toggle :selected
(and
(not
(listp idlwave-shell-show-commands))
(eq idlwave-shell-show-commands 'everything))]
(Everything menu-item "Everything" menu-function-112 :key-sequence nil :button
(:toggle and
(not
(listp idlwave-shell-show-commands))
(eq idlwave-shell-show-commands 'everything)))

(not
(eq idlwave-shell-show-commands 'everything))]
